We used to check for `self.tainted_by_errors()` to\n   206→                // avoid inundating the user with unnecessary errors, but we now\n   207→                // check upstream for type errors and don't add the obligations to\n   208→                // begin with in those cases.\n   209→                if matches!(\n   210→                    self.tcx.as_lang_item(trait_pred.def_id()),\n   211→                    Some(LangItem::Sized | LangItem::MetaSized)\n   212→                ) {\n   213→                    return match self.tainted_by_errors() {\n   214→                        None => self\n   215→                            .emit_inference_failure_err(\n   216→                                obligation.cause.body_id,\n   217→                                span,\n   218→                                trait_pred.self_ty().skip_binder().into(),\n   219→                                TypeAnnotationNeeded::E0282,\n   220→                                false,\n   221→                            )\n   222→                            .emit(),\n   223→                        Some(e) => e,\n   224→                    };\n   225→                }\n   226→\n   227→                // Typically, this ambiguity should only happen if\n   228→                // there are unresolved type inference variables\n   229→                // (otherwise it would suggest a coherence\n   230→                // failure). But given #21974 that is not necessarily\n   231→                // the case -- we can have multiple where clauses that\n   232→                // are only distinguished by a region, which results\n   233→                // in an ambiguity even when all types are fully\n   234→                // known, since we don't dispatch based on region\n   235→                // relationships.\n   236→\n   237→                // Pick the first generic parameter that still contains inference variables as the one\n   238→                // we're going to emit an error for. CandidateSource::DefId(did) => infcx.tcx.generics_of(*did).count() == 0,\n   283→                        CandidateSource::ParamEnv(_) => true,\n   284→                    }) {\n   285→           }\n   291→                }\n   292→                if ambiguities.len() > 1 && ambiguities.len() < 10 && has_non_region_infer {\n   293→                    if let Some(e) = &hir::PathSegment<'tcx>,\n        span: Span,\n        call_expr: &'tcx hir::Expr<'tcx>,\n        self_expr: &'tcx hir::Expr<'tcx>,\n    ) -> Result<MethodCallee<'tcx>, MethodError<'tcx>> {\n        let pick = self.lookup_probe_for_diagnostic(\n            segment.ident,\n            self_ty,\n            call_expr,\n            ProbeScope::TraitsInScope,\n            None,\n        )?;\n\n        Ok(self\n            .confirm_method_for_diagnostic(span, self_expr, call_expr, self_ty, &pick, segment)\n            .callee)\n    }\n\n    #[instrument(level = \"debug\", skip(self, call_expr))]\n    pub(crate) fn lookup_probe(\n        &self,\n        method_name: Ident,\n        self_ty: Ty<'tcx>,\n        call_expr: &hir::Expr<'_>,\n        scope: ProbeScope,\n    ) -> probe::PickResult<'tcx> {\n        let pick = self.probe_for_name(\n            probe::Mode::MethodCall,\n            method_name,\n            None,\n            IsSuggestion(false),\n            self_ty,\n            call_expr.hir_id,\n            scope,\n        )?;\n        pick.maybe_emit_unstable_name_collision_hint(self.tcx, method_name.span, call_expr.hir_id);\n        Ok(pick)\n    }\n\n    pub(crate) fn lookup_probe_for_diagnostic(\n        &self,\n        method_name: Ident,\n        self_ty: Ty<'tcx>,\n        call_expr: &hir::Expr<'_>,\n        scope: ProbeScope,\n        return_type: Option<Ty<'tcx>>,\n    ) -> probe::PickResult<'tcx> {\n        let pick = self.probe_for_name(\n            probe::Mode::MethodCall,\n            method_name,\n            return_type,\n            IsSuggestion(true),\n            self_ty,\n            call_expr.hir_id,\n            scope,\n        )?;\n        Ok(pick)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Used by [FnCtxt::lookup_method_for_operator] with `-Znext-solver`.\n///\n/// With `AsRigid` we error on `impl Opaque: NotInItemBounds` while\n/// `AsInfer` just treats it as ambiguous and succeeds. This is necessary\n/// as we want [FnCtxt::check_expr_call] to treat not-yet-defined opaque\n/// types as rigid to support `impl Deref<Target = impl FnOnce()>` and\n/// `Box<impl FnOnce()>`.\n///\n/// We only want to treat opaque types as rigid if we need to eagerly choose\n/// between multiple candidates. We otherwise treat them as ordinary inference\n/// variable to avoid rejecting otherwise correct code.\n#[derive(Debug)]\npub(super) enum TreatNotYetDefinedOpaques {\n    AsInfer,\n    AsRigid,\n}\n\nimpl<'a, 'tcx> FnCtxt<'a, 'tcx> {\n    /// `lookup_method_in_trait` is used for overloaded operators.\n    /// It does a very narrow slice of what the normal probe/confirm path does.\n    /// In particular, it doesn't really do any probing: it simply constructs\n    /// an obligation for a particular trait with the given self type and checks\n    /// whether that trait is implemented.\n    #[instrument(level = \"debug\", skip(self))]\n    pub(super) fn lookup_method_for_operator(\n        &self,\n        cause: ObligationCause<'tcx>,\n        method_name: Symbol,\n        trait_def_id: DefId,\n        self_ty: Ty<'tcx>,\n        opt_rhs_ty: Option<Ty<'tcx>>,\n        treat_opaques: TreatNotYetDefinedOpaques,\n    ) -> Option<InferOk<'tcx, MethodCallee<'tcx>>> {\n        // Construct a trait-reference `self_ty : Trait<input_tys>`\n        let args = GenericArgs::for_item(self.tcx, trait_def_id, |param, _| match param.kind {\n            GenericParamDefKind::Lifetime | GenericParamDefKind::Const { .. } => {\n                unreachable!(\"did not expect operator trait to have lifetime/const\")\n            }\n            GenericParamDefKind::Type { .. } => {\n                if param.index == 0 {\n                    self_ty.into()\n                } else if let Some(rhs_ty) = opt_rhs_ty {\n                    assert_eq!(param.index, 1, \"did not expect >1 param on operator trait\");\n                    rhs_ty.into()\n                } else {\n                    // FIXME: We should stop passing `None` for the failure case\n                    // when probing for call exprs. I.e. `opt_rhs_ty` should always\n                    // be set when it needs to be.\n                    self.var_for_def(cause.span, param)\n                }\n            }\n        });\n\n        let obligation = traits::Obligation::new(\n            self.tcx,\n            cause,\n            self.param_env,\n            ty::TraitRef::new_from_args(self.tcx, trait_def_id, args),\n        );\n\n        // Now we want to know if this can be matched\n        let matches_trait = match treat_opaques {\n            TreatNotYetDefinedOpaques::AsInfer => self.predicate_may_hold(&obligation),\n            TreatNotYetDefinedOpaques::AsRigid => {\n                self.predicate_may_hold_opaque_types_jank(&obligation)\n            }\n        };\n\n        if !matches_trait {\n            debug!(\"--> Cannot match obligation\");\n            // Cannot be matched, no such method resolution is possible.\n            return None;\n        }\n\n        // Trait must have a method named `m_name` and it should not have\n        // type parameters or early-bound regions.\n        let tcx = self.tcx;\n        // We use `Ident::with_dummy_span` since no built-in operator methods have","numLines":200,"startLine":200,"totalLines":577}}}
